 Vimānavatthu 
  
  page      
   
 Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa  
   ITTHIVIMĀNA 
   ITTHIVIMĀNA 
 I PĪṬHAVAGGA 
   Paṭhamapīṭhavimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Pīṭhaṃ  te  sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 manojavaṃ gacchati yena kāmaṃ 
 alaṅkate malyadhare  suvatthe 
 obhāsasi vijju r iv  abbhakūṭaṃ           
 Vv I         Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā          
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti          
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena  pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ          
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 abbhāgatān  āsanakaṃ  adāsiṃ 
 abhivādayiṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ 
 yathānubhāvañ ca adāsi dānaṃ          
 Vv I         Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā          
 Vv I         Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti          
 Paṭhamapīṭhavimānaṃ  
  
                                                                            R T pīṭhan te  Variants due to different styles of orthography 
 will not be noted generally  The replacement of v with b in B  
 also followed by N  e g  sahabyatā  byākāsi  etc  will not be 
 noted generally  
   T mālya    S  malla  R  kūtaṃ 
    K  Moggalānena  throughout  
   C   VvA C   gatānaṃ āsanakaṃ 
   B N add paṭhamaṃ  E T Pīṭhavimānaṃ paṭhamaṃ

   Itthivimāna 
   Dutiyapīṭhavimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Pīṭhaṃ te veḷuriyamayaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 manojavaṃ gacchati yena kāmaṃ 
 alaṅkate malyadhare  suvatthe 
 obhāsasi vijju r iv  abbhakūṭaṃ          
 Vv I         Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā          
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 abbhāgatān  āsanakaṃ  adāsiṃ 
 abhivādayiṃ añjalikaṃ akāsiṃ 
 yathānubhāvañ ca adāsi dānaṃ           
 Vv I         Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Dutiyapīṭhavimānaṃ

   B N add dutiyaṃ  R T Pīṭhavimānaṃ dutiyaṃ 
  
  page      
   Pīṭhavagga 
   Tatiyapīṭhavimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Pīṭhaṃ te sovaṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 manojavaṃ gacchati yena kāmaṃ 
 alaṅkate malyadhare  suvatthe 
 obhāsasi vijju r iv  abbhakūṭaṃ           
 Vv I         Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I          Appassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ  
 yen  amhi  evaṃ jalitānubhāvā           
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 purimāya jātiyā manussaloke  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ vippasannam anāvilaṃ 
 tassa adās  ahaṃ  pīṭhaṃ pasannā sehi  pāṇihi            
 Vv I         Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Tatiyapīṭhavimānaṃ  
  
                                                                            T mālya    S  malla   M  omits these two lines  Almost all editions viz  R C B N VvA 
 add the first two lines of the next verse to these two lines to 
 make up a trisṭubh stanza  
    K  mam  etaṃ 
    K  ten  amhi 
   T adāsi haṃ 
   R T sakehi pāṇihi  B N sehi pāṇibhi 
   B N add tatiyaṃ  R T Pīṭhavimānaṃ tatiyaṃ

   Itthivimāna 
   Catutthapīṭhavimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Pīṭhaṃ te veḷuriyamayaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 manojavaṃ gacchati yena kāmaṃ 
 alaṅkate malyadhare  suvatthe 
 obhāsasi vijju r iv  abbhakūṭaṃ           
 Vv I         Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I          Appassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ 
 yen  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā           
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 purimāya jātiyā manussaloke  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ bhikkhuṃ vippasannam anāvilaṃ 
 tassa adās  ahaṃ  pīṭhaṃ pasannā sehi  pāṇihi            
 Vv I         Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Akkhāmi te  bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam  akāsi puññaṃ  
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Catutthapīṭhavimānaṃ  
  
                                                                            T mālya    S  malla  Vide No    n    regarding the arrangement of this verse  
   T adāsi haṃ 
   R T sakehi pāṇihi  B N sehi pāṇibhi 
   R T taṃ 
   R T yam ahaṃ akāsiṃ 
   B N add catutthaṃ  R T Pīṭhavimānaṃ catutthaṃ 
  
  page      
   Pīṭhavagga 
   Kuñjaravimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Kuñjaro te varāroho nānāratanakappano 
 ruciro  thāmavā javasampanno  ākāsamhi samīhati           
 Vv I         Padumī padmapattakkhī  padm  uppalajutindharo  
 padmacuṇṇābhikiṇṇaṅgo  soṇṇapokkharamālavā            
 Vv I         Padumānusaṭaṃ  maggaṃ padmapattavibhūsitaṃ  
 ṭhitaṃ vaggum anugghāti  mitaṃ gacchati vāraṇo           
 Vv I         Tassa pakkamamānassa soṇṇakaṃsā  ratissarā  
 tesaṃ suyyati nigghoso turiye  pañcaṅgike yatha           
 Vv I         Tassa nāgassa khandhasmiṃ  sucivatthā alaṅkatā 
 mahantaṃ accharāsaṅghaṃ vaṇṇena atirocasi            
 Vv I         Dānassa te idaṃ phalaṃ atho sīlassa vā pana 
 atho añjalikammassa taṃ me akkhāhi pucchitā ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I         Disvāna guṇasampannaṃ jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ sataṃ 
 adāsiṃ pupphābhikiṇṇaṃ āsanaṃ dussasanthataṃ           
 Vv I         Upaḍḍhaṃ    padmamālāhaṃ   āsanassa samantato 
 abbhokirissaṃ pattehi pasannā sehi   pāṇihi             
 Vv I          Tassa kammassa   kusalassa   idaṃ me īdisaṃ   phalaṃ 
 sakkāro garukāro ca devānaṃ apacitā ahaṃ           
 Vv I          Yo ve sammāvimuttānaṃ santānaṃ brahmacārinaṃ 
 pasanno āsanaṃ dajjā evaṃ nande yathā ahaṃ           
 Vv I          Tasmā hi attakāmena   mahattam   abhikaṅkhatā 
 āsanaṃ dātabbaṃ hoti sarīrantimadhārinan ti           
 Kuñjaravimānaṃ   
  
                                                                            C    in fn  mention a rdg  in  B   ruciyo thāmasampanno  
 The probable correct rdg  is ruciro javasampanno  vv vv     
 although thāmavā had been includes in the pāda at least as 
 early as the  th c  A C  as seen in VvA  
   C    T VvA C  padum a    throughout  
   R T sovaṇṇa    G   māladhā 
   R T  satam 
   B N  ghātī 
   R T sovaṇṇakaṃ sāratissarā 
   B tūriye  throughout ū  
   R T B N khandhamhi 
    S   rocati 
    R T upaḍḍhapadumālāhaṃ  C    VvA C  upaḍḍhapadumamālāhaṃ  
  M   G  upaddhaṃ paddhamālāhaṃ 
    R T sakehi pāṇihi  B N sehi pāṇibhi 
    R T B N kamma kusalassa 
    R T tādisaṃ 
    VvA C  attha   R mahattham 
    R T B N add pañcamaṃ

   Itthivimāna 
   Paṭhamanāvāvimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ nāvaṃ nāri āruyha tiṭṭhasi 
 ogāhasi  pokkharaṇiṃ padmaṃ  chindasi pāṇinā            
 Vv I          Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 purimāya jātiyā manussaloke 
 disvāna bhikkhū tasite kilante 
 uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ           
 Vv I         Yo ve kilantāna  pipāsitānaṃ 
 uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti 
 sītodakā  tassa bhavanti najjo 
 pahūtamalyā  bahupuṇḍarīkā           
 Vv I         Tam āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā 
 sītodakā  vālukasanthatā nadī 
 ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo 
 uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā

   Pīṭhavagga 
 Vv I         Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ 
 vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusa sobhamānaṃ 
 tassīdha  kammassa ayaṃ vipāko 
 etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti           
 Vv I          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I          Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

   Dutiyanāvāvimānavatthu

 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jahitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ

   Itthivimāna 
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 purimāya jātiyā manussaloke 
 disvāna bhikkhuṃ tasitaṃ kilantaṃ 
 uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ           
 Vv I         Yo ve kilantassa pipāsitassa 
 uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti 
 sītodakā  tassa bhavanti najjo 
 pahūtamalyā   bahupuṇḍarīkā            
 Vv I         Tam āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā 
 sītodakā  vālukasanthatā nadī 
 ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo 
 uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā           
 Vv I         Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ 
 vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusa sobhamānaṃ 
 tassīdha  kammassa ayaṃ vipāko 
 etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti           
 Vv I          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I          Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Dutiyanāvāvimānaṃ  
    
   Tatiyanāvāvimānavatthu

  page      
   Pīṭhavagga 
 Vv I         Kūṭāgārā nivesā te vibhattā bhāgaso mitā 
 daddallamānā ābhanti samantā caturo disā           
 Vv I         Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā sambuddhen  eva pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 purimāya jātiyā manussaloke 
 disvāna bhikkhū tasite kilante 
 uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ adāsiṃ           
 Vv I         Yo ve kilantāna  pipāsitānaṃ 
 uṭṭhāya pātuṃ udakaṃ dadāti 
 sītodakā  tassa bhavanti najjo 
 pahūtamalyā  bahupuṇḍarīkā           
 Vv I         Tam āpagā anupariyanti sabbadā 
 sītodakā  vālukasanthatā nadī 
 ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo 
 uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā           
 Vv I         Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ 
 vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bhusa sobhamānaṃ 
 tassīdha  kammassa ayaṃ vipāko 
 etādisaṃ puññakatā labhanti           
 Vv I          Kūṭāgārā nivesā me vibhattā bhāgaso mitā 
 daddallamānā ābhanti samantā caturo disā           
 Vv I          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I           Ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsati 
 Etassa kammassa phalaṃ  mamedaṃ  
 atthāya  buddho udakaṃ apāyī ti             
 Tatiyanāvāvimanaṃ   
  
                                                                            T ogāḷhasi 
   C      T  VvA C  padumaṃ 
   VvA R  kilantānaṃ 
   C      VvA C  sītodikā 
    M  bahutta malyā 
   R  T tass  eva 
   B  N add here the hemistich  
 Akkhāmi te buddha mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam akāsi puññaṃ  
  M  has the above hemistich and pādas a  b of v      
   R  T ayaṃ vipāko 
   R  T uṭṭhāya 
    R  T apāsī ti 
    B  N add aṭṭhamaṃ  R  T Nāvāvimānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ

    Itthivimāna 
   Dīpavimānavatthu 
 Vv I         Abhikkantena vaṇṇena yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate 
 obhāsentī disā sabbā osadhī viya tārakā           
 Vv I         Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā           
 Vv I         Kena tvaṃ vimalobhāsā atirocasi devate 
 kena te sabbagattehi sabbā obhāsate  disā           
 Vv I         Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti           
 Vv I         Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ           
 Vv I         Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 purimāya jātiyā manussaloke 
 tamandhakāramhi timīsikāyaṃ 
 padīpakālamhi adaṃ  padīpaṃ            
 Vv I         Yo andhakāramhi timīsikāyaṃ 
 padīpakālamhi dadāti  dīpaṃ 
 uppajjati jotirasaṃ vimānaṃ 
 pahūtamalyaṃ bahupuṇḍarīkaṃ

 Dutiyapatibbatāvimānaṃ  
  
                                                                            There is a confusion in the division into verses in 
 the various editions  B N VvA C  add these two lines 
 to v    and R to v     VvA R  is not acceptable  
 Here I follow C   
   B N add ca 
   R T nāpi 
   C    VvA C   K  abhāsiṃ 
   C    VvA C  sāminā va 
   VvA R  and  B  omit this hemistich 
   R T yam ahaṃ akāsiṃ 
   R T B N add dvādasamaṃ

    Sirimāvimānavatthu 
 Vv I           Yuttā ca te parama alaṅkatā hayā 
 adhomukhā aghasigamā balī javā 
 abhinimmitā pañcarathāsatā ca te 
 anventi taṃ sārathicoditā hayā            
 Vv I           Sā tiṭṭhasi rathavare alaṅkatā 
 obhāsayaṃ jalam iva jotipāvako 
 pucchāmi taṃ varatanu  anomadassane  
 kasmā nu  kāyā anadhivaraṃ upāgamī ti             
 Vv I           Kāmaggappattānaṃ yam āhu  anuttaraṃ  
 nimmāya nimmāya ramanti devatā 
 tasmā kāyā accharā kāmavaṇṇinī  
 idhāgatā anadhivaraṃ  namassituṃ             
 Vv I           Kiṃ tvaṃ pure sucaritam ācarīdha  
 ken  acchasi   tvaṃ amitayasā sukhedhitā 
 iddhī ca te anadhivarā vihaṅgamā 
 vaṇṇo ca te dasadisā virocati            
 Vv I           Devehi tvaṃ parivutā   sakkatā   c  asi 
 kuto cutā sugatigatāsi devate 
 kassa vā tvaṃ vacanakarānusāsaniṃ   
 ācikkha me tvaṃ yadi buddhasāvikā ti              
 Vv I           Nagantare nagaravare sumāpite 
 paricārikā rājavarassa   sirīmato 
 nacce   gīte   paramasusikkhitā ahuṃ   
 Sirimā ti maṃ Rājagahe avediṃsu            
 Vv I           Buddho ca me isinisabho   vināyako 
 adesayī   samudayadukkhaniccataṃ 
 asaṅkhataṃ dukkhanirodhasassataṃ   
 maggañ c  imam akuṭilam añjasaṃ sivaṃ            
 Vv I           Sutvān  ahaṃ amatapadam asaṅkhataṃ 
 tathāgatass  anadhivarassa   sāsanaṃ 
  sīlesv  ahaṃ  paramasusaṃvutā ahuṃ 
 dhamme ṭhitā naravarabuddhadesite              
 Vv I           Ñatvān  ahaṃ   virajapadaṃ   asaṅkhataṃ 
 tathāgaten  anadhivarena desitaṃ 
 tatth  ev  ahaṃ samathasamādhim āphusiṃ 
 sā yeva me paramaniyāmatā ahu

 II CITTALATAVĀGGA 
    Dāsivimānavatthu 
 Vv II          Api Sakko va devindo ramme Cittalatāvane 
 samantā anupariyāsi nārīgaṇapurakkhatā  
 obhāsentī disā sabbā osadhī viya tārakā            
 Vv II          Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv II          Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti            
 Vv II          Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ            
 Vv II          Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūtā 
 dāsī ahosiṃ parapessiyā  kule  
  upāsikā cakkhumato Gotamassa yasassino            
 Vv II          Tassā me nikkamo āsi sāsane tassa tādino  
 kāmaṃ bhijjatu yaṃ kāyo n  eva atth  ettha 
 santhanaṃ            
 Vv II          Sikkhāpadānaṃ pañcannaṃ maggo sovatthiko sivo 
 akaṇṭako agahaṇo  uju sabbhi pavedito            
 Vv II          Nikkamassa phalaṃ passa yath  idaṃ pāpuṇ  itthikā 
 āmantanikā rañño mhi  Sakkassa vasavattino

    Lakhumāvimānavatthu 
 Vv II           Abhikkantena vaṇṇena yā tvaṃ tiṭṭhasi devate 
 obhāsentī disā sabbā osadhī viya tārakā            
 Vv II          Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv II          Pucchāmi taṃ devi mahānubhāve 
 manussabhūtā kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti            
 Vv II          Sā devatā attamanā Moggallānena pucchitā 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭhā viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ            
 Vv II          Kevaṭṭadvārā nikkhamma ahu mayhaṃ nivesanaṃ 
 tattha sañcaramānānaṃ  sāvakānam mahesinaṃ            
 Vv II          Odanaṃ kummāsaṃ  ḍākaṃ  loṇasovīrakañ c  ahaṃ 
 adāsiṃ ujubhūtesu vippannena cetasā            
 Vv II          Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yā  ca  pakkhassa aṭṭhamī 
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañ ca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ           
 Vv II          Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ  sadā sīlesu saṃvutā 
  saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca vimānaṃ āvasām  ahaṃ            
 Vv II          Pāṇātipātā viratā musāvādā ca saññatā 
 theyyā ca aticārā ca majjapānā ca ārakā           
 Vv II           Pañcasikkhāpade ratā ariyasaccāna kovidā 
 upāsikā cakkhumato Gotamassa yasassino            
 Vv II           Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv II           Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūtā yam ahaṃ akāsiṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti            
 Mama ca bhante vacanena bhagavato pāde sirasā 
 vandeyyāsi  Lakhumā nāma bhante upāsikā bhagavato pāde 
 sirasā vandatī ti  Anacchariyaṃ kho pan  etaṃ bhante

 yaṃ maṃ bhagavā aññatarasmiṃ sāmaññaphale vyākareyya

    Ācāmadāyikāvimānavatthu 
 Vv II          Piṇḍāya  te carantassa tuṇhībhūtassa tiṭṭhato 
 daliddā  kapaṇā nārī parāgāram avassitā             
 Vv II          Yā te adāsi ācāmaṃ pasannā sehi  pāṇihi  
 sā hitvā mānusaṃ  dehaṃ kaṃ nu sā  disataṃ  gatā            
 Vv II          Piṇḍāya me carantassa tuṇhībhūtassa tiṭṭhato 
 daliddā  kapaṇā nārī parāgāram avassitā             
 Vv II          Yā me adāsi ācāmaṃ pasannā sehi  pāṇihi  
 sā hitvā mānusaṃ  dehaṃ vippamuttā ito cutā            
 Vv II          Nimmānaratino  nāma santi devā mahiddhikā 
 tattha sā sukhitā nārī modat  ācāmadāyikā             
 Vv II          Aho dānaṃ varākiyā  Kassape suppatiṭṭhitaṃ 
 parābhatena   dānena ijjhittha vata dakkhiṇā            
 Vv II          Yā mahesittaṃ kāreyya cakkavattissa rājino 
 nārī sabbaṅgakalyāṇī bhattu cānomadassikā    
 etassācāmadānassa kalaṃ nāgghati   soḷasiṃ            
 Vv II          Sataṃ nikkhā sataṃ assā sataṃ assatarīrathā   
 sataṃ kaññāsahassāni āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā 
 etassācāmadānassa kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ            
 Vv II          Sataṃ Hemavatā nāgā īsādantā   urūḷhavā 
 suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā   
 etassācāmadānassa kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ

                                                                          Preliminary note  
 There is an error in the numbering of verses in R  the 
 verses numbered                 the un numbered hemistich 
 after it      to     should read                         
 to     respectively  Both B and N have numbered the 
 verses correctly          making a total of      VvA R  
 leaves out the repeated verses and numbers the rest        
 The Sinhalese editions and T do not number them  B  N 
 give sub headings to each one of the    episodes in the story  
          Vatthuttamadāyikāvimānavatthu

           Gandhuttamadāyikā v v            
           Phaluttamadāyikā v v            
           Rasuttamadāyikā v v            
           Gandhapañcaṅgulikadāyikā v v            
           Ekūposatha v v            
           Udakadāyikā v v            
           Upaṭṭhāna v v            
            Aparakammakārinī   v v            
            Khīrodanadāyikā v v            
            Phāṇita d v v            
             Ucchukhaṇḍika   d v v            
              Timbarūsaka d v v            
              Kakkārika d v v

   Anantaraṃ   pañcavīsativimānaṃ yathā Khīrodanadāyikāvimānaṃ   tathā vitthāretabbaṃ  
  The same formula as before in cycles of eight verses 
 viz                       etc  is repeated twenty five 
 times with the fifth verse viz             etc  in each 
 cycle  mentioning in its first word the gift given  It 
 runs   
         ahaṃ adāsiṃ 
 bhikkhuno piṇḍāya carantassa 
 evaṃ karitvā kammaṃ 
 sugatiṃ uppajja modāmi  
  The following words should be used to fill the blank 
 in the preceding verse and the verses so formed should be 
 numbered as below

 Vv III          Daddallamānā  vaṇṇena yasasā  ca yasassinī 
 sabbe deve Tāvatiṃse vaṇṇena atirocasi            
 Vv III          Dassanaṃ nābhijānāmi idaṃ paṭhamadassanaṃ 
 kasmā kāyā nu āgamma nāmena bhāsase maman ti            
 Vv III          Ahaṃ bhadde Subhaddāsiṃ pubbe mānusake bhave 
 sahabhariyā ca te āsiṃ bhaginī ca kaniṭṭhikā             
 Vv III          Sāhaṃ  kāyassa bhedāya  vippamuttā tato cutā 
 Nimmānaratidevānaṃ  upapannā sahavyatan ti            
 Vv III          Pahūtakatakalyāṇā te deve yanti pāṇino 
 yesaṃ tvaṃ kittayissasi Subhadde jātim attano            
 Vv III          Kathaṃ  tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena kena vā anusāsitā 
 kīdisen  eva dānena subbatena yasassinī           
 Vv III          Yasaṃ etādisaṃ pattā visesaṃ  vipulam ajjhatā 
 devate pucchitācikkha kissa kammass  idaṃ phalan 
 ti             
 Vv III          Aṭṭh  eva piṇḍapātāni yaṃ dānaṃ adadaṃ pure 
 dakkhiṇeyyassa saṅghassa pasannā sehi  pāṇihi             
 Vv III          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati

 manussabhūtā yam ahaṃ akāsiṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvā 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

 tappesiṃ annapānena pasannā sehi  pāṇihi  
   tayā bahutaraṃ datvā hīnakāyūpagā ahaṃ              
 Vv III           Kathaṃ tvaṃ appataraṃ datvā visesaṃ vipulam 
 ajjhagā 
 devate pucchitācikkha kissa kammass  idaṃ phalan 
 ti

 Vv III           Manobhāvaniyo bhikkhu sandiṭṭho me pure ahu 
 tāhaṃ bhattena   nimantesiṃ Revataṃ atta naṭṭhamaṃ            
 Vv III           So me atthapurekkhāro   anukampāya Revato  
 saṅghe dehī ti maṃ voca   tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ kariṃ            
 Vv III           Sā dakkhiṇā saṅghagatā appameyye   patiṭṭhitā  
 puggalesu tayā dinnaṃ na taṃ tava mahapphalan ti            
 Vv III           Idān  evāhaṃ jānāmi saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ 
 sāhaṃ gantvā manussattaṃ vadaññū vītamaccharā 
 saṅghe dānāni   dassāmi   appamattā punappunan ti            
 Vv III           Kā esā devatā bhadde tayā mantayate   saha 
 sabbe deve Tāvatiṃse vaṇṇena atirocatī ti             
 Vv III           Manussabhūtā devinda pubbe mānusake bhave 
 sahabhariyā ca me āsi bhaginī ca kaniṭṭhikā 
 saṅghe dānāni datvāna katapuññā virocatī ti             
 Vv III           Dhammena pubbe   bhaginī   tayā bhadde virocati   
 yaṃ saṅghamhi   appameyye   patiṭṭhāpesi 
 dakkhiṇaṃ            
 Vv III           Pucchito hi mayā buddho Gijjhakūṭamhi   pabbate 
 vipākaṃ saṃvibhāgassa yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ            
 Vv III           Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ 
 karotaṃ   opadhikaṃ puññaṃ yattha dinnaṃ 
 mahapphalaṃ            
 Vv III           Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi jānaṃ kammaphalaṃ sakaṃ 
 vipākaṃ saṃvibhāgassa yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ            
 Vv III           Cattāro ca paṭipannā cattāro ca phale ṭhitā 
 esa saṅgho ujubhūto paññāsīlasamāhito

 es  appameyyo udadhīva sāgaro 
 ete hi seṭṭhā naravīrasāvakā   
 pabhaṅkarā dhammam   udīrayanti

 Vv III          Phaḷikarajatahemajālacchannaṃ 
 vividhavicitratalam  addasaṃ surammaṃ 
 vyamhaṃ sunimmitaṃ toraṇūpapannaṃ 
 rucakupakiṇṇam  idaṃ subhaṃ vimānaṃ

 sarade tamonudo  sahassaraṃsī 
 tathā tapati m idaṃ tava vimānaṃ 
 jalam iva dhūmasikho nise  nabhagge             
 Vv III          Musatīva nayanaṃ sateratā  va 
 ākāse ṭhapitam idaṃ manuññaṃ 
 vīṇāmurajasammatāḷaghuṭṭhaṃ 
 iddhaṃ Indapuraṃ yathā tavedaṃ             
 Vv III          Padumakumuduppalakuvalayaṃ  
 yodhikabandhukanojakā  ca santi

 vividhadumaggasugandhasevitam idaṃ

 kusakasuphullitalatāvalambinīhi   
 maṇijālasadisā   yasassinī 
 rammā pokkharaṇī upaṭṭhitā te            
 Vv III          Udakaruhā ca ye tthi pupphajātā 
 thalajā   ye ca   santi rukkhajātā 
 mānusakā   amānusakā   ca dibbā 
 sabbe   tuyhaṃ nivesanamhi jātā            
 Vv III          Kissa samadamass  ayaṃ   vipāko 
 kenāsi   kammaphalen  idhūpapannā 
 yathā ca   te adhigatam idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 tad anupadaṃ avacāsi lārapakhume   ti            
 Vv III          Yathā ca   me adhigatam idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 koñcamayūracakorasaṅghacaritaṃ

 pāṭalijambuasokarukkhavantaṃ 
 yathā ca me adhigatam idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 tan te pavedissāmi   suṇohi bhante

 saddhā sīlena sampannā saṃvibhāgaratā sadā            
 Vv III          Acchādanañ ca bhattañ ca senāsanaṃ padīpiyaṃ

 theyyā ca aticārā ca majjapānā ca ārakā           
 Vv III          Pañcasikkhāpade ratā ariyasaccāna kovidā 
 upāsikā cakkhumato Gotamassa yasassino

 aññe mahiddhikatarā mayā devā ti

 Vv IV           Ghāyase taṃ sucigandhaṃ rūpaṃ passasi amānusaṃ   
 devate pucchitācikkha kissa kammass  idaṃ 
 phalan ti            
 Vv IV           Dāsī ahaṃ pure āsiṃ Gayāyaṃ brāhmaṇass   ahaṃ   
 appapuññā alakkhikā Rajjumālā ti maṃ vidū              
 Vv IV           Akkosānaṃ vadhānañ ca tajjanāya ca ukkatā   
 kuṭaṃ gahetvā nikkhamma gacchiṃ   udakahāriyā              
 Vv IV            Vipathe kuṭaṃ nikkhipitvā vanasaṇḍaṃ   upāgamiṃ  
 idh  evāhaṃ marissāmi kvattho   pi   jīvitena me            
 Vv IV            Daḷhaṃ   pāsaṃ karitvāna āsumbhitvāna   pādape 
 tato disā vilokesiṃ  ko   nu kho vanam assito              
 Vv IV            Tatth  addasāsiṃ   sambuddhaṃ sabbalokahitaṃ 
 muniṃ   
 nisinnaṃ rukkhamūlasmiṃ jhāyantaṃ akutobhayaṃ            
 Vv IV            Tassā me ahu   saṃvego abbhuto   lomahaṃsano  
 ko   nu kho vanam assito   manusso udāhu devatā            
 Vv IV            Pāsādikaṃ pasādanīyaṃ   vanā nibbanam   āgataṃ 
 disvā mano me pasīdi  nāyaṃ yādisak  īdiso              
 Vv IV            Guttindriyo jhānarato abahiggatamānaso   
 hito sabbassa lokassa buddho so yaṃ   bhavissati            
 Vv IV            Bhayabheravo durāsado sīho va guham assito   
 dullabhāyaṃ dassanāya pupphaṃ odumbaraṃ   yathā            
 Vv IV            So maṃ mudūhi vācāhi ālapitvā tathāgato 
 Rajjumāle ti maṃ voca   saraṇaṃ gaccha tathāgataṃ            
 Vv IV            Tāhaṃ giraṃ suṇitvāna nelaṃ   atthavatiṃ suciṃ   
 saṇhaṃ muduñ ca vagguñ ca sabbasokāpanūdanaṃ              
 Vv IV            Kallacittañ ca maṃ ñatvā pasannaṃ suddhamānasaṃ 
 hito sabbassa lokassa anusāsi tathāgato            
 Vv IV            Idaṃ dukkhan ti maṃ voca   ayaṃ dukkhassa sambhavo 
 ayaṃ   nirodho maggo ca   añjaso amatogadho            
 Vv IV            Anukampakassa kusalassa ovādamhi ahaṃ ṭhitā

 Vv IV            Sāhaṃ avaṭṭhitā pemā dassane avikampinī 
 mūlajātāya saddhāya dhītā buddhassa orasā

   PURISAVIMĀNA 
 V MAHĀRATHAVAGGA 
    Maṇḍūkadevaputtavimānavatthu 
 Vv V          Ko me vandati pādāni iddhiyā yasasā jalaṃ 
 abhikkantena vaṇṇena sabbā obhāsayaṃ disā ti            
 Vv V          Maṇḍūko  haṃ  pure āsiṃ udake vārigocaro 
 tava dhammaṃ suṇantassa avadhī  vacchapālako            
 Vv V          Muhuttaṃ cittappasādassa  iddhiṃ passa yasañ ca me 
 ānubhāvañ ca me passa vaṇṇaṃ passa jutiñ ca me            
 Vv V          Ye ca te dīgham addhānaṃ dhammaṃ assosuṃ Gotama 
 pattā te acalaṭṭhānaṃ  yattha gantvā na socare ti            
 Maṇḍūkadevaputtavimānaṃ  
    
    Revatīvimānavatthu 
 Vv V          Cirappavāsiṃ purisam dūrato sotthim āgataṃ 
 ñātimittā suhajjā ca abhinandanti āgataṃ            
  
                                                                             
   R Maṇḍūko ahaṃ   M  Maṇḍuko haṃ 
   R  T  VvA R  avadhi 
   R  T  B  N cittapasādassa 
    M  acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ 
   R  T  B  N add paṭhamaṃ 
  
  page      
    Purisavimāna 
 Vv V          Tath  eva katapuññam pi asmā lokā paraṃ gataṃ 
 puññāni paṭigaṇhanti  piyaṃ ñātī  va āgataṃ            
 Vv V          Uṭṭhehi Revate supāpadhamme 
 āparutaṃ  dvāraṃ  adānasīle 
 nessāma taṃ yattha thunanti duggatā 
 samappitā nerayikā dukkhenā ti             
 Vv V          Icc eva  vatvāna Yamassa dūtā 
 te dve yakkhā lohitakkhā brahantā 
 paccekabāhāsu gahetvā  Revatiṃ  
 pakkāmayuṃ  devagaṇassa santike            
 Vv V          Ādiccavaṇṇaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ 
 vyamhaṃ subhaṃ kañcanajālachannaṃ 
 kass  etam ākiṇṇajanaṃ vimānaṃ 
 suriyassa raṃsī r iva   jotamānaṃ            
 Vv V          Nārīgaṇā candanasāralittā   
 ubhato vimānaṃ upasobhayanti 
 taṃ dissati suriyasamānavaṇṇaṃ 
 ko modati saggappatto   vimāne ti            
 Vv V          Bārāṇasiyaṃ Nandiyo nāmāsi upāsako 
 amaccharī dānapatī vadaññū  
 tass  etam ākiṇṇajanaṃ vimānaṃ 
 suriyassa raṃsī r iva   jotamānaṃ            
 Vv V          Nārīgaṇā   candanasāralittā   
 ubhato vimānaṃ upasobhayanti 
 taṃ dissati suriyasamānavaṇṇaṃ 
 so modati saggappatto   vimāne ti            
 Vv V          Nandiyassāhaṃ bhariyā 
 agārinī sabbakulassa issarā 
 bhattu vimāne ramissāmi dān  ahaṃ   
 na patthaye nirayaṃ   dassanāyā ti              
 Vv V           Eso   te nirayo supāpadhamme 
 puññaṃ tayā akataṃ jīvaloke 
 na hi maccharī   rosako pāpadhammo 
 saggūpagānaṃ labhati   sahavyatan ti            
 Vv V           Kin nu gūthañ ca muttañ ca asucī   paṭidissati 
 duggandhaṃ kim idaṃ mīḷhaṃ   kim etaṃ upavāyatī 
 ti              
 Vv V           Esa Saṃsavako nāma   gambhīro sataporiso 
 yattha vassasahassāni tuvaṃ paccasi Revate ti            
  
                                                                           
  page      
    Mahārathavagga 
 Vv V           Kin nu kāyena vācāya manasā dukkataṃ   kataṃ 
 kena Saṃsavako laddho   gambhīro sataporiso ti              
 Vv V           Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi aññe vā   pi vanibbake   
 musāvādena vañcesi   taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ tayā            
 Vv V           Tena Saṃsavako laddho gambhīro sataporiso 
 tattha vassasahassāni tuvaṃ paccasi Revate            
 Vv V           Hatthe pi chindanti atho pi pāde 
 kaṇṇe pi chindanti atho pi nāsaṃ 
 atho pi kākoḷagaṇā samecca 
 saṅgamma khādanti viphandamānan ti            
 Vv V           Sādhu kho maṃ paṭinetha kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ 
 dānena samacariyāya saññamena   damena ca 
 yaṃ katvā sukhitā honti na ca pacchānutappare ti            
 Vv V           Pure tvaṃ pamajjitvā idāni paridevasi 
 sayaṃ katānaṃ kammānaṃ vipākaṃ anubhossasī ti              
 Vv V           Ko devalokato manussalokaṃ 
 gantvāna puṭṭho me evaṃ vadeyya  
 nikkhittadaṇḍesu dadātha dānaṃ 
 acchādanaṃ sayanam   ath  annapānaṃ 
 na hi maccharī   rosako pāpadhammo 
 saggūpagānaṃ labhati   sahavyatan ti            
 Vv V             Sāhaṃ nūna ito gantvā yoniṃ laddhāna mānusiṃ 
 vadaññū sīlasampannā kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ 
 dānena samacariyāya saññamena   damena ca            
 Vv V           Ārāmāni ca ropissaṃ dugge saṅkamanāni ca 
 papañ ca udapānañ ca vippasannena cetasā            
 Vv V           Cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī 
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañ ca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ           
 Vv V           Uposathaṃ upavasissaṃ sadā sīlesu saṃvutā 
 na ca dāne pamajjissaṃ sāmaṃ diṭṭhaṃ idaṃ mayā ti            
 Vv V           Icc evaṃ vippalapantiṃ   phandamānaṃ tato tato 
 khipiṃsu niraye ghore uddhapādaṃ   avaṃsiraṃ            
 Vv V           Ahaṃ pure maccharinī ahosiṃ 
 paribhāsikā sumaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ 
 vitathena sāmikaṃ vañcayitvā 
 paccām  ahaṃ niraye ghorarūpe ti            
 Revatīvimānaṃ

    Chattamāṇavakavimānavatthu 
 Vv V          Yo vadataṃ pavaro manujesu 
 Sakyamunī  bhagavā katakicco 
 pāragato balaviriya  samaṅgī 
 taṃ sugataṃ saraṇattham upehi            
 Vv V          Rāgavirāgam anejam  asokaṃ 
 dhammam asaṅkhatam appaṭikūlaṃ 
 madhuram imaṃ paguṇaṃ suvibhattaṃ 
 dhammam imaṃ saraṇattham upehi            
  
                                                                            VvA R  Sakyamuni 
    M  valavīra      VvA R  balavīra  T  aneñja 
  page      
    Mahārathavagga 
 Vv V          Yattha ca dinnamahapphalam āhu 
 catusu  sucīsu purisayugesu 
 aṭṭha ca puggaladhammadasā  te 
 saṅgham imaṃ saraṇattham upehi            
 Vv V          Na tathā tapati nabhasmiṃ  suriyo  
 cando ca  na bhāsati na phusso 
 yathātulam  idaṃ mahappabhāsaṃ 
 ko nu tvaṃ Tidivā mahiṃ upāgā              
 Vv V          Chindati ca   raṃsi   pabhaṅkarassa   
 sādhikavīsativojanāni   ābhā 
 rattim pi ca   yathā   divaṃ karoti 
 parisuddhaṃ vimalaṃ subhaṃ vimānaṃ            
 Vv V          Bahupadumavicitrapuṇḍarīkaṃ   
 vokiṇṇaṃ kusumehi nekacittaṃ   
 arajavirajahemajālacchannaṃ   
 ākāse tapati yathā pi suriyo             
 Vv V          Rattambarapītavāsasāhi   
 agarupiyaṅgucandanussadāhi   
 kañcanatanusannibhattacāhi 
 paripūraṃ gaganaṃ   va tārakāhi            
 Vv V          Naranāriyo   bahuk  ettha nekavaṇṇā 
 kusumavibhūsitābharaṇ  ettha   sumanā   
 anilapamuñcitā   pavanti   surabhiṃ    
 tapanīyavitatā   suvaṇṇacchādanā              
 Vv V          Kissa saṃyamassa   ayaṃ vipāko 
 kenāsi kammaphalen  idhūpapanno 
 yathā ca te adhigatam idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 tad anupadaṃ   avacāsi   iṅgha puṭṭho ti            
 Vv V           Yam   idha pathe samecca māṇavena 
 satthānusāsi   anukampamāno 
 tava   ratanavarassa dhammaṃ sutvā 
 karissāmī ti   ca   bravittha Chatto            
 Vv V           Jinavarapavaraṃ   upemi   saraṇaṃ 
 dhammañ cāpi tath  eva bhikkhusaṅghaṃ  
 no ti paṭhamaṃ avocāhaṃ   bhante 
 pacchā te vacanaṃ tath  ev  akāsiṃ            
 Vv V           Mā ca pāṇavadhaṃ vividhaṃ carassu   asuciṃ 
 na hi pāṇesu asaññataṃ avaṇṇayiṃsu sappaññāno ti paṭhamaṃ avocāhaṃ   bhante 
 pacchā te vacanaṃ tath  ev  akāsiṃ

    Purisavimāna 
 Vv V             Mā ca parajanassa rakkhitam   pi   
 ādātabbam amaññittha   adinnaṃ 
 no ti paṭhamaṃ avocāhaṃ   bhante 
 pacchā te vacanaṃ tath  ev  akāsiṃ            
 Vv V           Mā ca parajanassa rakkhitāyo 
 parabhariyā   agamā anariyam   etaṃ 
 no ti paṭhamaṃ avocāhaṃ   bhante 
 pacchā te vacanaṃ tath  ev  akāsiṃ            
 Vv V           Mā ca vitathaṃ aññathā abhāṇi   
 na hi musāvādaṃ avaṇṇayiṃsu sapaññā 
 no ti paṭhamaṃ avocāhaṃ   bhante 
 pacchā te vacanaṃ tath  ev  akāsiṃ            
 Vv V           Yena ca purisassa apeti saññā 
 taṃ majjaṃ   parivajjayassu sabbaṃ 
 no ti paṭhamaṃ avocāhaṃ   bhante 
 pacchā te vacanaṃ tath  ev  akāsiṃ            
 Vv V           Svāhaṃ idha pañca sikkhā karitvā 
 paṭipajjitvā tathāgatassa dhamme 
 dvepatham agamāsiṃ coramajjhe 
 te maṃ tattha vadhiṃsu bhogahetu            
 Vv V           Ettakam idaṃ anussarāmi kusalaṃ 
 tato paraṃ na me vijjati aññaṃ 
 tena sucaritena kammunāhaṃ 
 upapanno   Tidivesu kāmakāmī            
 Vv V           Passa khaṇamuhuttasaññamassa 
 anudhammapaṭipattiyā   vipākaṃ 
 jalam iva yasasā samekkhamānā   
 bahukā   maṃ pihayanti hīnakāmā              
 Vv V           Passa katipayāya desanāya 
 sugatiñ c  amhi gato sukhañ ca patto 
 ye ca   te satataṃ   suṇanti dhammaṃ 
 maññe te amataṃ phusanti khemaṃ            
 Vv V           Appakam pi   kataṃ mahāvipākaṃ 
 vipulaṃ hoti   tathāgatassa dhamme 
 passa katapuññatāya Chatto 
 obhāseti paṭhaviṃ   yathā pi suriyo             
 Vv V           Kim idaṃ kusalaṃ ācarema 
 icc eke hi samecca mantayanti 
 te   mayaṃ punar eva   laddha   mānusattaṃ 
 paṭipannā viharemu   sīlavanto

 Vv V          Uccam idaṃ maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ 
 samantato dvāvasayojanāni 
 kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā 
 veḷuriyatthambhā  rucakatthatā  subhā

    Mahārathavagga 
 Vv V          Tatth  acchasi  pivasi khādasī  ca 
 dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vaggū  
 dibbā rasā kāmaguṇ  ettha pañca 
 nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā             
 Vv V          Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv V          Pucchāmi taṃ deva mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto  kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo  
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti            
 Vv V          So devaputto attamano Moggallānena pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho   viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ 
 phalaṃ            
 Vv V          Satisamuppādakaro dvāre kakkaṭako ṭhito 
 niṭṭhito jātarūpassa sobhati dasapādako            
 Vv V          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv V            Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

    Nāgavimānavatthu  
 Vv V           Susukkakhandhaṃ abhiruyha nāgaṃ 
 ākācinaṃ  dantiṃ  baliṃ mahājavaṃ 
 āruyha gajavaraṃ  sukappitaṃ 
 idhāgamā vehāsayam  antalikkhe            
 Vv V           Nāgassa dantesu duvesu nimmitā 
 acchodikā  paduminiyo suphullā 
 padumesu ca turiyagaṇā  pavajjare  
 imā ca naccanti manoharāyo            
 Vv V           Deviddhipatto si mahānubhāvo 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti            
 Vv V           So devaputto attamano Moggallānena pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ            
 Vv V           Aṭṭh  eva muttapupphāni  Kassapassa mahesino   
 thūpasmiṃ abhiropesiṃ   pasanno sehi   pāṇihi              
 Vv V           Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv V           Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

    Dutiyanāgavimānavatthu 
 Vv V           Mahantaṃ nāgaṃ abhiruyha sabbasetaṃ gajuttamaṃ 
 vanā  vanaṃ  anupariyāsi nārīgaṇapurakkhato  
 obhāsento disā sabbā osadhī viya tārakā            
 Vv V           Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā            
 Vv V           Pucchāmi taṃ deva mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti            
 Vv V           So devaputto attamano Moggallānena pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ phalaṃ            
 Vv V           Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto 
 upāsako cakkhumato ahosiṃ 
 pāṇātipātā virato ahosiṃ 
 loke adinnaṃ parivajjayissaṃ            
 Vv V           Amajjapo na ca musā abhāṇiṃ  
 sakena dārena ca tuṭṭho ahosiṃ 
 annañ ca pānañ ca pasannacitto 
 sakkacca  dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ

 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā

 manussabhūto yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

 Vv V           Ko nu dibbena yānena sabbasetena hatthinā 
 turiyatāḷitanigghoso  antalikkhe  mahīyati             
 Vv V           Devatā nu si gandhabbo ādu  Sakko purindado 
 ajānantā taṃ pucchāma kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayan ti            
 Vv V           N  amhi devo na gandhabbo nāpi  Sakko purindado 
 Sudhammā nāma ye devā tesaṃ aññataro ahan ti            
 Vv V           Pucchāma devaṃ  Sudhammaṃ  puthuṃ katvāna añjaliṃ 
 kiṃ katvā mānuse kammaṃ Sudhammaṃ upapajjatī ti

 tiṇṇam aññataraṃ datvā Sudhammaṃ upapajjatī ti

 migaṃ  tañ c  eva  nāddakkhiṃ tañ ca disvā ṭhito

    Mahārathavagga 
 Vv V           Svāgataṃ te mahāpuñña atho te adurāgataṃ  
 etto  udakam ādāya pāde pakkhālayassu te            
 Vv V           Idam pi pāniyaṃ  sītaṃ ābhataṃ girigabbharā 
 rājaputta tato pītvā   santhatasmiṃ upāvisā ti            
 Vv V           Kalyāṇī   vata te vācā savaṇīyā   mahāmuni 
 nelā   atthavatī   vaggu   mantā   atthañ ca 
 bhāsasi              
 Vv V           Kā   te rati vane viharato   
 isinisabha vadehi puṭṭho 
 tava vacanapathaṃ nisāmayitvā 
 atthadhammapadaṃ samācaremase ti            
 Vv V           Ahiṃsā sabbapāṇīnaṃ kumār  amhāka   ruccati 
 theyyā ca aticārā ca majjapānā ca ārati            
 Vv V           Ārati   samacariyā ca bāhusaccaṃ kataññutā 
 diṭṭh  eva dhamme pāsaṃsā   dhammā ete pasaṃsiyā 
 ti            
 Vv V            Santike maraṇaṃ tuyhaṃ oraṃ māsehi pañcahi 
 rājaputta vijānāhi attānaṃ parimocayā ti            
 Vv V            Katamaṃ svāhaṃ janapadaṃ gantvā kiṃ kammaṃ 
 kiñ ca   porisaṃ 
 kāya vā pana vijjāya bhaveyyaṃ ajarāmaro ti            
 Vv V            Na vijjate so   padeso   kammaṃ vijjā ca porisaṃ 
 yattha gantvā bhave macco rājaputtājarāmaro              
 Vv V            Mahaddhanā mahābhogā raṭṭhavanto pi khattiyā 
 pahūtadhanadhaññāse te   pi na   ajarāmarā            
 Vv V            Yadi te sutā Andhakaveṇhuputtā   
 sūrā vīrā vikkantappahārino 
 te pi āyukkhayaṃ   pattā 
 viddhastā sassatī   samā              
 Vv V            Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā suddā caṇḍālapukkusā 
 ete c  aññe ca jātiyā te   pi na   ajarāmarā            
 Vv V            Ye mantaṃ parivattenti   chaḷaṅgaṃ brahmacintitaṃ 
 ete c  aññe ca vijjāya   te   pi no   ajarāmarā            
 Vv V            Isayo cāpi ye santā saññatattā tapassino 
 sarīraṃ te pi kālena vijahanti tapassino

 Vv V            Bhāvitattā pi arahanto katakiccā anāsavā 
 nikkhipanti imaṃ dehaṃ puññapāpaparikkhayā ti              
 Vv V            Subhāsitā atthavatī gāthāyo te mahāmuni 
 nijjhatto mhi subhaṭṭhena tvañ ca me saraṇaṃ 
 bhavā ti            
 Vv V            Mā maṃ tvaṃ saraṇaṃ gaccha tam eva saraṇaṃ vaja   
 Sakyaputtaṃ mahāvīraṃ yam ahaṃ saraṇaṃ gato ti            
 Vv V            Katarasmiṃ so janapade satthā tumhāka mārisa 
 aham pi daṭṭhuṃ gacchissaṃ jinaṃ appaṭipuggalan 
 ti            
 Vv V            Puratthimasmiṃ janapade Okkākakulasambhavo 
 satthāsi   purisājañño so ca kho parinibbuto ti            
 Vv V            Sace hi buddho tiṭṭheyya satthā tumhāka mārisa 
 yojanāni sahassāni gaccheyyaṃ   payirupāsituṃ            
 Vv V            Yato ca   kho    parinibbuto  satthā tumhāka mārisa 
 nibbutam pi   mahāvīraṃ gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ            
 Vv V            Upemi saraṇaṃ buddhaṃ dhammañ cāpi anuttaraṃ 
 saṅghañ ca naradevassa gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ            
 Vv V            Pāṇātipātā viramāmi khippaṃ 
 loke adinnaṃ parivajjayāmi 
 amajjapo no ca musā bhaṇāmi 
 sakena dārena ca homi tuṭṭho ti             
 Vv V            Sahassaraṃsīva yathā mahappabho 
 disaṃ yathā bhāti nabhe anukkamaṃ 
 tathappakāro   tav  ayaṃ   mahāratho 
 samantato yojanasatta m āyato               
 Vv V            Suvaṇṇapaṭṭehi samantam otthaṭo   
 ur  assa muttāhi maṇīhi cittito 
 lekhā suvaṇṇassa ca rūpiyassa ca   
 sobhanti   veḷuriyamayā sunimmitā             
 Vv V            Sīsañ c  idaṃ veḷuriyassa nimmitaṃ 
 yugañ c  idaṃ lohitakāya cittitaṃ 
 yuttā   suvaṇṇassa ca rūpiyassa ca 
 sobhanti assā ca   p  ime   manojavā             
 Vv V            So tiṭṭhasi hemarathe adhiṭṭhito 
 devānam indo va sahassavāhano 
 pucchāmi tāhaṃ yasavanta kovidaṃ 
 kathaṃ tayā laddho ayaṃ uḷāro ti

 purindado bhūtapatīva Vāsavo

 suvaṇṇarājīhi atīva saṅgataṃ 
 veḷuriyarājiva   atīva sobhati             
 Vv V           Ime ca vāḷī   maṇicandakappitā   
 ārohakambū sujavā brahūpamā   
 brahā mahantā balino mahājavā 
 mano tav  aññāya tath  eva siṃsare               
 Vv V           Ime ca sabbe sahitā catukkamā 
 mano tav  aññāya tath  eva siṃsare   
 samaṃ vahantā   mudukā anuddhatā 
 āmodamānā turagānam   uttamā             
 Vv V           Dhunanti   vagganti   patanti   c  ambare   
 abbhuddhunantā   sukate pilandhane   
 tesaṃ saro suyyati   vaggurūpo   
 pañcaṅgikaṃ turiyam iva ppavāditaṃ               
 Vv V            Rathassa ghoso apilandhanāna   ca   
 khurassa nādo   abhihiṃsanāya   ca 
 ghoso suvaggū samitassa   suyyati   
 gandhabbaturiyāni   vicitrasaṃvane

 āḷārapamhā hasitā piyaṃvadā 
 veḷuriyajālāvatatā   tanucchavā 
 sad  eva gandhabbasuraggapūjitā               
 Vv V            Tā   rattarattambarapītavāsasā   
 visālanettā abhirattalocanā 
 kule   sujātā   sutanū sucimhitā   
 rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā             
 Vv V            Tā   kambukāyuradharā   suvāsasā   
 sumajjhimā ūruthan  ūpapannā

 rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā

 samaṃ vibhattāhi pabhassarāhi ca 
 anubbatā   tā tava mānase ratā 
 rathe ṭhitā pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā

 alaṅkatā candanasāravāsitā

 obhāsayantī   dasa sabbaso   disā

 bhujesu mālā apilandhanāni   ca 
 muñcanti ghosaṃ ruciraṃ suciṃ subhaṃ 
 sabbehi viññūhi sutabbarūpaṃ

 rathā ca nāgā turiyāni   ca ssaro

 mahīyamāno vajirāvudho r iva

 yaṃ devasaṅghaṃ abhirocase bhusaṃ

 atho añjalikammassa taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito ti

 avāpurantaṃ   amatassa dvāraṃ 
 devātidevaṃ satapuññalakkhaṇaṃ             
 Vv V            Tam addasaṃ kuñjaram oghatiṇṇaṃ 
 suvaṇṇasiṅgīnadabimbasādisaṃ   
 disvāna taṃ khippam ahuṃ sucīmano   
 tam eva disvāna subhāsitaddhajaṃ             
 Vv V            Tamh  annapānaṃ   athavā pi cīvaraṃ 
 suciṃ   paṇitaṃ rasasā upetaṃ 
 pupphābhikiṇṇamhi sake nivesane   
 patiṭṭhapesiṃ   sa asaṅgamānaso               
 Vv V            Tam annapānena ca cīvarena ca 
 khajjena bhojjena ca sāyanena ca 
 santappayitvā dvipadānam   uttamaṃ  
 so saggaso devapure ramām  ahaṃ             
 Vv V            Eten  upāyena imaṃ niraggaḷaṃ 
 yaññaṃ yajitvā tividhaṃ visuddhaṃ 
 pahāy  ahaṃ mānusakaṃ   samussayaṃ 
 Indūpamo   devapure ramām  ahaṃ             
 Vv V            Āyuñ ca vaṇṇañ ca sukhaṃ balañ ca 
 paṇītarūpaṃ   abhikaṅkhatā muni 
 annañ ca pānañ ca bahuṃ susaṅkhataṃ 
 patiṭṭhapetabbam   asaṅgamānase               
 Vv V            Na   y imasmim   loke parasmiṃ vā pana 
 buddhena seṭṭho va   samo va   vijjati 
 āhuneyyānaṃ paramāhutiṃ   gato 
 puññatthikānaṃ   vipulapphalesinan ti             
 Mahārathavimānaṃ

 VI  PĀYĀSIVAGGA 
    Agāriyavimānavatthu  
 Vv VI          Yathā vanaṃ Cittalataṃ pabhāsati 
 uyyānaseṭṭhaṃ Tidasānam uttamaṃ 
 tathūpamaṃ tuyham idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe              
 Vv VI          Deviddhipatto si mahānubhāvo 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
 Vv VI          So devaputto attamano Moggallānena  pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ 
 phalaṃ             
 Vv VI          Ahañ ca bhariyā ca manussaloke 
 opānabhūtā  gharam āvasimha  
 annañ ca pānañ ca pasannacittā 
 sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adamha             
 Vv VI          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā             
 Vv VI          Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatīti             
 Agāriyavimānaṃ  
  
                                                                            B  N paṭhama agāriya  C      VvA C  antaḷikkhe

   R opanabhūtā 
   R  T āvasimhā 
   R  T add paṭhamaṃ  B  N paṭhama agāraya  paṭhamaṃ

     Pāyāsivagga 
    Phaladāyakavimānavatthu 
 Vv VI          Uccam idaṃ maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ 
 samantato soḷasa  yojanāni 
 kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā 
 veḷuriyatthambhā  rucakatthatā  subhā             
 Vv VI          Tatth  acchasi pivasi khādasī  ca 
 dibbā  ca vīṇā pavadanti  vaggū  
 aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā 
 dibbā ca kaññā Tidasacarā  uḷārā 
 naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti             
 Vv VI          Deviddhipatto si mahānubhāvo 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
 Vv VI          So devaputto attamano Moggallānena pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ 
 phalaṃ             
 Vv VI          Phaladāyī phalaṃ vipulaṃ labhati 
 dadam ujjugatesu  pasannamānaso 
 so   hi modati   saggagato   Tidive   
 anubhoti   ca puññaphalaṃ vipulaṃ  
 tath  evāham   mahāmuni adāsiṃ caturo phale             
 Vv VI          Tasmā hi phalaṃ alam eva dātuṃ 
 niccaṃ manussena sukhatthikena 
 dibbāni vā patthayatā sukhāni 
 manussasobhaggatam   icchatā vā               
 Vv VI          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā             
 Vv VI          Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

    Uttaravimānavatthu  
 Vv VI           Yā devarājassa sabhā Sudhammā 
 yatth  acchati  devasaṅgho samaggo 
 tathūpamaṃ tuyham idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe              
 Vv VI           Dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vaggū 
 aṭṭhaṭṭhakā sikkhitā sādhurūpā 
 dibbā ca kaññā Tidasacarā uḷārā 
 naccanti gāyanti pamodayanti             
 Vv VI           Deviddhipatto si mahānubhāvo 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
 Vv VI           Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto 
 rañño Pāyāsissa ahosiṃ  māṇavo 
 laddhā dhanaṃ saṃvibhāgaṃ akāsiṃ 
 piyā ca me sīlavanto ahesuṃ 
 annañ ca pānañ ca pasannacitto 
 sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ             
 Vv VI           Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā

 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
 Uttaravimānaṃ  
    
 Tass  uddānaṃ  
 Dve agārino phaladāyī dve upassayadāyī bhikkhāya  
 yavapālako c  eva dve kuṇḍalino  Pāyāsī ti   
 Purisavimāne dutiyo vaggo 
 PĀYĀSIVAGGO CHAṬṬHO

 Uttara to this vatthu though the chapter is throughout 
 called Pāyāsivagga  B  N Pāyāsivimānavatthu

 VII SUNIKKHITTAVAGGA 
    Cittalatāvimānavatthu 
 Vv VII          Yathā vanaṃ Cittalataṃ pabhāsati 
 uyyānaseṭṭhaṃ Tidasānam uttamaṃ 
 tathūpamaṃ tuyham idaṃ vimānaṃ 
 obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati antalikkhe              
 Vv VII          Deviddhipatto si mahānubhāvo 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
 Vv VII          So devaputto attamano Moggallānena pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ 
 phalaṃ             
 Vv VII          Ahaṃ manussesu manussabhūto 
 daliddo  atāṇo kapaṇo kammakaro ahosiṃ 
 jiṇṇe ca mātāpitaro abhāriṃ  
 piyā ca me sīlavanto ahesuṃ 
 annañ ca pānañ ca pasannacitto 
 sakkacca dānaṃ vipulaṃ adāsiṃ             
 Vv VII          Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā             
 Vv VII          Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto yam akāsi puññaṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti

    Maṭṭakuṇḍalī  vimānavatthu 
 Vv VII          Alaṅkato maṭṭakuṇḍalī  
 mālādhārī  haricandanussado 
 bāhā  paggayha kandasi 
 vanamajjhe kiṃ dukkhito tuvan ti             
 Vv VII          Sovaṇṇamayo pabhassaro 
 uppanno rathapañjaro mama 
 tassa cakkayugaṃ na vindāmi 
 tena dukkhena jahissaṃ  jīvitan ti             
 Vv VII          Sovaṇṇamayaṃ maṇimayaṃ 
 lohitaṅkamayaṃ  atha rūpiyāmayaṃ  
 ācikkha  me  bhadda māṇava  
 cakkayugaṃ paṭilābhayāmi  te   ti             
 Vv VII          So māṇavo tassa pāvadi  
 candasuriyā   ubhay  ettha dissare   
 sovaṇṇamayo ratho mama 
 tena cakkayugena sobhatī ti             
 Vv VII          Bālo kho tvam asi   māṇava 
 yo   tvaṃ patthayase   apatthiyaṃ 
 maññāmi tuvaṃ   marissasi 
 na hi   tuvaṃ   lacchasi candasūriye   ti             
 Vv VII          Camanāgamanam pi dissati 
 vaṇṇadhātu ubhayattha   vīthiyā   
 peto pana   kālakato   na   dissati 
 ko n  idha   kandataṃ bālyataro   ti             
 Vv VII          Saccaṃ kho vadesi māṇava 
 aham eva kandataṃ bālyataro   
 candaṃ viya dārako rudaṃ 
 petaṃ kālakatābhipatthayan   ti             
 Vv VII          Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ ghatasittaṃ va pāvakaṃ 
 vārinā viya osiñcaṃ   sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ             
 Vv VII          Abbahī   vata me sallaṃ sokaṃ   hadayanissitaṃ 
 yo me sokaparetassa puttasokaṃ apānudi

     Purisavimāna 
 Vv VII           Svāhaṃ   abbūḷhasallo smi sītibhūto smi   
 nibbuto   
 na socāmi na rodāmi tava sutvāna māṇavā ti             
 Vv VII           Devatā nu si gandhabbo ādu   Sakko purindado 
 ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ 
 mayan ti             
 Vv VII           Yañ ca   kandasi yañ ca rodasi 
 puttaṃ āḷāhane   sayaṃ ḍahitvā   
 svāhaṃ kusalaṃ karitvā   kammaṃ 
 Tidasānaṃ sahavyataṃ patto   ti             
 Vv VII           Appaṃ vā bahuṃ vā nāddasāma   
 dānaṃ dadantassa sake agāre 
 uposathakammaṃ vā tādisaṃ 
 kena kammena gato si devalokan ti             
 Vv VII           Ābādhiko haṃ dukkhito gilāno   
 āturarūpo   mhi sake nivesane 
 buddhaṃ vigatarajaṃ vitiṇṇakaṅkhaṃ 
 addakkhiṃ sugataṃ anomapaññaṃ             
 Vv VII           Svāhaṃ muditamano pasannacitto 
 añjaliṃ akariṃ tathāgatassa 
 tāhaṃ kusalaṃ karitvāna   kammaṃ 
 Tidasānaṃ sahavyataṃ patto   ti               
 Vv VII           Acchariyaṃ vata abbhūtaṃ   
 añjalikammassa   ayam īdiso vipāko 
 aham pi muditamano pasannacitto 
 ajj  eva buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ vajāmī ti             
 Vv VII           Ajj  eva buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ vahāhi 
 dhammañ ca saṅghañ ca pasannacitto 
 tath  eva sikkhāya padāni pañca 
 akhaṇḍaphullāni samādiyassu             
 Vv VII           Pāṇātipātā viramassu khippaṃ 
 loke adinnaṃ parivajjayassu 
 amajjapo mā   ca musā bhaṇāhi 
 sakena dārena ca hohi tuṭṭho             
 Vv VII           Atthakāmo si me yakkha hitakāmo si devate 
 karomi tuyhaṃ vacanaṃ tvaṃ si ācariyo mama             
 Vv VII           Upemi buddhaṃ   saraṇaṃ   dhammañ cāpi anuttaraṃ 
 saṅghañ ca naradevassa gacchāmi saraṇaṃ ahaṃ

 Vv VII           Suṇotha  yakkhassa ca vāṇijāna ca 
 samāgamo yattha tadā ahosi 
 yathā kathaṃ itarītarena  cāpi 
 subhāsitaṃ tañ ca suṇātha  sabbe             
 Vv VII           Yo so ahu rājā Pāyāsi nāma  
 Bhummānaṃ sahavyagato yasassī 
 so modamāno va sake vimāne 
 amānuso mānuse ajjhabhāsī ti             
 Vv VII           Vaṅke  araññe amanussaṭṭhāne  
 kantāre appodake appabhakkhe 
 suduggame vaṇṇupathassa  majjhe 
 vaṅkaṃbhayā  naṭṭhamanā manussā             
 Vv VII           Na y idha phalā mūlamayā ca santi 
 upādānaṃ natthi kuto dha bhakkho  
 aññatra paṃsūhi ca vālukāhi ca 
 tattāhi   uṇhāhi ca dāruṇāhi ca             
 Vv VII           Ujjaṅgalaṃ tattaṃ ivaṃ   kapālaṃ 
 anāyasaṃ   paralokena tulyaṃ

 bhūmippadeso abhisattarūpo

 kim āsamānā   imaṃ padesaṃ   hi

 lobhā bhayā athavā sampamūḷhā ti

 āropayissaṃ   paṇiyaṃ   puthuttaṃ   
 te yāmase Sindhu Sovīrabhūmiṃ 
 dhanatthikā uddayaṃ   patthayānā

 suduggame vaṇṇupathassa  majjhe 
 disaṃ na jānāma pamūḷhacittā

 vimānaseṭṭhañ ca tavañ ca   yakkha

 disvā patītā sumanā udaggā ti

 verajjake mānuse pekkhamānā 
 yaṃ vo sutaṃ vā   athavā pi diṭṭhaṃ

 sakehi kammehi apāpakehi

 yassānukampāya idhāgato si 
 lābhā hi tassa yassa tuvaṃ   pihesī ti

     Sunikkhittavagga 
 Vv VII            Yo kappako Sambhavanāmadheyyo 
 upāsako kocchaphalūpajīvī   
 jānātha naṃ tumhākaṃ pesiyo   so 
 mā   kho naṃ hīḷittha supesalo so ti             
 Vv VII            Jānāmase yaṃ tvaṃ vadesi   yakkha 
 na kho naṃ    jānāma    sa    ediso    ti 
 mayam pi naṃ pūjayissāma yakkha 
 sutvāna tuyhaṃ vacanaṃ uḷāran ti             
 Vv VII            Ye kec  imasmiṃ    satthe    manussā 
 daharā mahantā athavā pi majjhimā 
 sabbe va te ālambantu    vimānaṃ 
 passantu puññāna    phalaṃ kadariyā ti             
 Vv VII            Te tattha sabbe va  ahaṃ pure ti 
 taṃ kappakaṃ tattha purakkhipitvā    
 sabbe va te ālaṃbiṃsu    vimānaṃ 
 Masakkasāraṃ viya Vāsavassa             
 Vv VII            Te tattha sabbe va  ahaṃ pure ti 
 upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayiṃsu    
 pāṇātipātā viratā ahesuṃ 
 loke adinnaṃ parivajjayiṃsu 
 amajjapā no ca musā bhaṇiṃsu 
 sakena dārena ca    ahesuṃ tuṭṭhā             
 Vv VII            Te tattha sabbe va  ahaṃ pure ti 
 upāsakattaṃ paṭivedayitvā   pakkāmi sattho    anumodamāno 
 yakkhiddhiyā anumato punappunaṃ             
 Vv VII            Gantvāna te Sindhu Sovīrabhūmiṃ 
 dhanatthikā uddayaṃ    patthayānā 
 yathāpayogā paripuṇṇalābhā 
 paccāgamuṃ Pāṭaliputtam    akkhataṃ             
 Vv VII            Gantvāna te saṃ gharaṃ sotthivanto 
 puttehi dārehi samaṅgibhūtā 
 ānandī    vittā    sumanā patītā 
 akaṃsu Serissa   mahaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 Serissakaṃ    te    pariveṇaṃ māpayiṃsu             
 Vv VII            Etādisā sappurisāna sevanā 
 mahatthikā    dhammaguṇāna sevanā 
 ekassa atthāya upāsakassa 
 sabbe va sattā sukhitā    ahesun ti             
 Serissakavimānaṃ

     Purisavimāna 
    Sunikkhittavimānavatthu 
 Vv VII           Uccam  idaṃ maṇithūṇaṃ vimānaṃ 
 samantato dvādasayojanāni 
 kūṭāgārā sattasatā uḷārā 
 veḷuriyatthambhā  rucakatthatā  subhā             
 Vv VII           Tatth  acchasi pivasi khādasī  ca 
 dibbā ca vīṇā pavadanti vaggū  
 dibbā rasā kāmaguṇ  ettha pañca 
 nāriyo ca naccanti suvaṇṇachannā             
 Vv VII           Kena t  etādiso vaṇṇo kena te idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca te bhogā ye keci manaso piyā             
 Vv VII           Pucchāmi taṃ deva mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto kim akāsi puññaṃ 
 kenāsi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca te sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
  
                                                                           
  page      
     Sunikkhittavagga 
 Vv VII           So devaputto attamano Moggallānena pucchito 
 pañhaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi yassa kammass  idaṃ 
 phalaṃ             
 Vv VII           Dunikkhittaṃ mālaṃ sunikkhipitvā 
 patiṭṭhapetvā sugatassa thūpe 
 mahiddhiko c  amhi mahānubhāvo 
 dibbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto             
 Vv VII           Tena m  etādiso vaṇṇo tena me idha m ijjhati 
 uppajjanti ca me bhogā ye keci manaso piyā             
 Vv VII            Akkhāmi te bhikkhu mahānubhāva 
 manussabhūto yam ahaṃ akāsiṃ 
 ten  amhi evaṃ jalitānubhāvo 
 vaṇṇo ca me sabbadisā pabhāsatī ti             
 Sunikkhittavimānaṃ  
    
 Tass  uddānaṃ  
 Dve daliddā  dve  vihārā  bhatako  gopāla Kanthakā  
 anekavaṇṇa maṭṭakuṇḍalī  Serissako  sunikkhittaṃ  
 purisānaṃ tatiyo  vaggo  ti  
 Purisavimāne tatiyo vaggo 
 Bhāṇavāraṃ catutthaṃ 
 Vimānavatthu  niṭṭhitaṃ  
 SUNIKKHITTAVAGGO SATTAMO
